üîπ¬†Networking for AI workloads¬†that connects GPU clusters and data centers with ultra-low latency

üîπ¬†AI-powered cybersecurity¬†that can predict and prevent threats in real time

üîπ¬†Quantum-safe optical and IP networks¬†built for the massive data demands of AI

It‚Äôs clear we are at the start of an¬†AI supercycle¬†that will reshape industries, economies, and societies as profoundly as the internet did. Nokia is showing how trusted connectivity and responsible AI can unlock these opportunities while keeping us secure and sustainable.

As¬†Futurist in Residence with Nokia, I‚Äôm hugely excited to see these advances up close and to explore what they mean for the future.

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        attributed-text-segment-list__content-truncated" dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">What does it take to make closed-loop automation in telecom a reality? 

In the latest episode of Networked, <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/showcase/attbusiness/?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>AT&amp;T Business</a>‚Äôs <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/yigal-elbaz-b1372b1?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Yigal Elbaz</a> sits down with <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/raghavsahgal?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Raghav Sahgal</a> to discuss why moving to open, cloud-native networks is essential for enabling automation and AI-driven transformation. 

üé• Watch the full conversation to learn why openness is the key to shaping the future of telecom: <a class="link" href="https://nokia.ly/47nDIBQ?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://nokia.ly/47nDIBQ</a></p>

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Smarter. Greener. Faster. Ready for the future.  
Our research and standardization teams are designing 6G so that every signal, device, and connection uses less energy, without compromising on performance or security.  

They‚Äôre turning bold ideas into networks we can actually rely on. Experts <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/in/peter-vetter-a72b444?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Peter Vetter</a> and <a class="link" href="https://de.linkedin.com/in/peter-merz-062ab01?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Peter Merz</a> share more in their new blog: <a class="link" href="https://lnkd.in/egnQpfiE?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" rel="nofollow" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>https://lnkd.in/egnQpfiE</a>

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Farchitectingtomorrow&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#ArchitectingTomorrow</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fnokia6g&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Nokia6G</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fbelllabs&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#BellLabs</a></p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="feed-reshare-content__commentary">I was at Big Data LDN 2025 today in my role as Futurist in Residence at @Nokia. It‚Äôs one of Europe‚Äôs leading data and AI events, and three themes really stood out this year:
¬†
‚ú¶ Generative AI &amp; AI Agents
The conversation has moved beyond experimentation. Organisations are now exploring autonomous agents and GenAI systems that embed intelligence directly into workflows and applications.
¬†
‚ú¶ Data Strategy, Governance &amp; Leadership
AI success depends on clear strategy, strong governance, ethical oversight and C-level ownership. Companies are working hard to turn data and AI into real business value with the right guardrails.
¬†
‚ú¶ Modern Data Architecture &amp; Engineering
Real-time platforms, DataOps, observability and data-as-a-product are transforming how enterprises design and scale data systems for AI.
¬†
<a class="link" href="https://ca.linkedin.com/in/w-sean-kennedy?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card_reshare-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Sean Kennedy</a>, Head of @Nokia Bell Labs AI Research,¬†also presented a fascinating session on AI myths that hold companies back and how to move past them. I‚Äôll be sharing more on these myths, along with other exciting things Nokia is doing in AI, over the coming weeks.
¬†
Which trends do you think will shape the future of data and AI?
